<p class="line" name=speech62><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.149>Nay, yet there's more in this:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.150>I prithee, speak to me as to thy thinkings,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.151>As thou dost ruminate, and give thy worst of thoughts</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.152>The worst of words.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech63><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.153>Good my lord, pardon me:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.154>Though I am bound to every act of duty,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.155>I am not bound to that all slaves are free to.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.156>Utter my thoughts? Why, say they are vile and false;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.157>As where's that palace whereinto foul things</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.158>Sometimes intrude not? who has a breast so pure,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.159>But some uncleanly apprehensions</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.160>Keep leets and law-days and in session sit</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.161>With meditations lawful?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech64><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.162>Thou dost conspire against thy friend, Iago,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.163>If thou but think'st him wrong'd and makest his ear</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.164>A stranger to thy thoughts.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech65><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.165>I do beseech you--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.166>Though I perchance am vicious in my guess,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.167>As, I confess, it is my nature's plague</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.168>To spy into abuses, and oft my jealousy</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.169>Shapes faults that are not--that your wisdom yet,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.170>From one that so imperfectly conceits,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.171>Would take no notice, nor build yourself a trouble</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.172>Out of his scattering and unsure observance.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.173>It were not for your quiet nor your good,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.174>Nor for my manhood, honesty, or wisdom,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.175>To let you know my thoughts.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech66><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.176>What dost thou mean?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech67><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.177>Good name in man and woman, dear my lord,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.178>Is the immediate jewel of their souls:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.179>Who steals my purse steals trash; 'tis something, nothing;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.180>'Twas mine, 'tis his, and has been slave to thousands:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.181>But he that filches from me my good name</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.182>Robs me of that which not enriches him</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.183>And makes me poor indeed.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech68><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.184>By heaven, I'll know thy thoughts.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech69><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.185>You cannot, if my heart were in your hand;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.186>Nor shall not, whilst 'tis in my custody.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech70><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.187>Ha!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech71><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.188>O, beware, my lord, of jealousy;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.189>It is the green-eyed monster which doth mock</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.190>The meat it feeds on; that cuckold lives in bliss</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.191>Who, certain of his fate, loves not his wronger;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.192>But, O, what damned minutes tells he o'er</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.193>Who dotes, yet doubts, suspects, yet strongly loves!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech72><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.194>O misery!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech73><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.195>Poor and content is rich and rich enough,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.196>But riches fineless is as poor as winter</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.197>To him that ever fears he shall be poor.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.198>Good heaven, the souls of all my tribe defend</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.199>From jealousy!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech74><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.200>                  Why, why is this?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.201>Think'st thou I'ld make a lie of jealousy,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.202>To follow still the changes of the moon</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.203>With fresh suspicions? No; to be once in doubt</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.204>Is once to be resolved: exchange me for a goat,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.205>When I shall turn the business of my soul</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.206>To such exsufflicate and blown surmises,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.207>Matching thy inference. 'Tis not to make me jealous</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.208>To say my wife is fair, feeds well, loves company,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.209>Is free of speech, sings, plays and dances well;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.210>Where virtue is, these are more virtuous:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.211>Nor from mine own weak merits will I draw</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.212>The smallest fear or doubt of her revolt;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.213>For she had eyes, and chose me. No, Iago;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.214>I'll see before I doubt; when I doubt, prove;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.215>And on the proof, there is no more but this,--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.216>Away at once with love or jealousy!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech75><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.217>I am glad of it; for now I shall have reason</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.218>To show the love and duty that I bear you</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.219>With franker spirit: therefore, as I am bound,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.220>Receive it from me. I speak not yet of proof.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.221>Look to your wife; observe her well with Cassio;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.222>Wear your eye thus, not jealous nor secure:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.223>I would not have your free and noble nature,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.224>Out of self-bounty, be abused; look to't:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.225>I know our country disposition well;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.226>In Venice they do let heaven see the pranks</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.227>They dare not show their husbands; their best conscience</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.228>Is not to leave't undone, but keep't unknown.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech76><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.229>Dost thou say so?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech77><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.230>She did deceive her father, marrying you;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.231>And when she seem'd to shake and fear your looks,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.232>She loved them most.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech78><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.233>And so she did.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech79><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.234>Why, go to then;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.235>She that, so young, could give out such a seeming,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.236>To seal her father's eyes up close as oak-</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.237>He thought 'twas witchcraft--but I am much to blame;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.238>I humbly do beseech you of your pardon</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.239>For too much loving you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech80><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.240>I am bound to thee for ever.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech81><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.241>I see this hath a little dash'd your spirits.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech82><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.242>Not a jot, not a jot.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech83><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.243>I' faith, I fear it has.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.244>I hope you will consider what is spoke</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.245>Comes from my love. But I do see you're moved:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.246>I am to pray you not to strain my speech</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.247>To grosser issues nor to larger reach</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.248>Than to suspicion.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech84><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.249>I will not.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech85><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.250>          Should you do so, my lord,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.251>My speech should fall into such vile success</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.252>As my thoughts aim not at. Cassio's my worthy friend--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.253>My lord, I see you're moved.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech86><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.254>No, not much moved:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.255>I do not think but Desdemona's honest.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech87><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.256>Long live she so! and long live you to think so!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech88><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.257>And yet, how nature erring from itself,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech89><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.258>Ay, there's the point: as--to be bold with you--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.259>Not to affect many proposed matches</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.260>Of her own clime, complexion, and degree,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.261>Whereto we see in all things nature tends--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.262>Foh! one may smell in such a will most rank,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.263>Foul disproportion thoughts unnatural.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.264>But pardon me; I do not in position</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.265>Distinctly speak of her; though I may fear</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.266>Her will, recoiling to her better judgment,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.267>May fall to match you with her country forms</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.268>And happily repent.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech90><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.269>Farewell, farewell:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.270>If more thou dost perceive, let me know more;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.271>Set on thy wife to observe: leave me, Iago:</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech91><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.272>[Going]  My lord, I take my leave.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech92><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.273>Why did I marry? This honest creature doubtless</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.274>Sees and knows more, much more, than he unfolds.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech93><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.275>[Returning]  My lord, I would I might entreat</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.276>your honour</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.277>To scan this thing no further; leave it to time:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.278>Though it be fit that Cassio have his place,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.279>For sure, he fills it up with great ability,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.280>Yet, if you please to hold him off awhile,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.281>You shall by that perceive him and his means:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.282>Note, if your lady strain his entertainment</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.283>With any strong or vehement importunity;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.284>Much will be seen in that. In the mean time,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.285>Let me be thought too busy in my fears--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.286>As worthy cause I have to fear I am--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.287>And hold her free, I do beseech your honour.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech94><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.288>Fear not my government.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech95><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.289>I once more take my leave.</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech96><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.290>This fellow's of exceeding honesty,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.291>And knows all qualities, with a learned spirit,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.292>Of human dealings. If I do prove her haggard,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.293>Though that her jesses were my dear heartstrings,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.294>I'ld whistle her off and let her down the wind,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.295>To pray at fortune. Haply, for I am black</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.296>And have not those soft parts of conversation</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.297>That chamberers have, or for I am declined</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.298>Into the vale of years,--yet that's not much--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.299>She's gone. I am abused; and my relief</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.300>Must be to loathe her. O curse of marriage,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.301>That we can call these delicate creatures ours,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.302>And not their appetites! I had rather be a toad,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.303>And live upon the vapour of a dungeon,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.304>Than keep a corner in the thing I love</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.305>For others' uses. Yet, 'tis the plague of great ones;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.306>Prerogatived are they less than the base;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.307>'Tis destiny unshunnable, like death:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.308>Even then this forked plague is fated to us</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.309>When we do quicken. Desdemona comes:</p>
<p><i>Re-enter DESDEMONA and EMILIA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.310>If she be false, O, then heaven mocks itself!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.311>I'll not believe't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech97><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.312>How now, my dear Othello!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.313>Your dinner, and the generous islanders</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.314>By you invited, do attend your presence.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech98><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.315>I am to blame.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech99><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.316>                  Why do you speak so faintly?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.317>Are you not well?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech100><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.318>I have a pain upon my forehead here.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech101><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.319>'Faith, that's with watching; 'twill away again:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.320>Let me but bind it hard, within this hour</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.321>It will be well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech102><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.322>                  Your napkin is too little:</p>
<p><i>He puts the handkerchief from him; and it drops</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.323>Let it alone. Come, I'll go in with you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech103><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.324>I am very sorry that you are not well.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt OTHELLO and DESDEMONA</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech104><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.325>I am glad I have found this napkin:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.326>This was her first remembrance from the Moor:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.327>My wayward husband hath a hundred times</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.328>Woo'd me to steal it; but she so loves the token,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.329>For he conjured her she should ever keep it,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.330>That she reserves it evermore about her</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.331>To kiss and talk to. I'll have the work ta'en out,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.332>And give't Iago: what he will do with it</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.333>Heaven knows, not I;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.334>I nothing but to please his fantasy.</p>
<p><i>Re-enter Iago</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech105><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.335>How now! what do you here alone?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech106><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.336>Do not you chide; I have a thing for you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech107><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.337>A thing for me? it is a common thing--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech108><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.338>Ha!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech109><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.339>To have a foolish wife.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech110><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.340>O, is that all? What will you give me now</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.341>For the same handkerchief?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech111><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.342>What handkerchief?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech112><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.343>What handkerchief?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.344>Why, that the Moor first gave to Desdemona;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.345>That which so often you did bid me steal.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech113><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.346>Hast stol'n it from her?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech114><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.347>No, 'faith; she let it drop by negligence.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.348>And, to the advantage, I, being here, took't up.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.349>Look, here it is.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech115><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.350>                  A good wench; give it me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech116><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.351>What will you do with 't, that you have been</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.352>so earnest</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.353>To have me filch it?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech117><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.354>[Snatching it]  Why, what's that to you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech118><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.355>If it be not for some purpose of import,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.356>Give't me again: poor lady, she'll run mad</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.357>When she shall lack it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech119><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.358>Be not acknown on 't; I have use for it.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.359>Go, leave me.</p>
<p><i>Exit EMILIA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.360>I will in Cassio's lodging lose this napkin,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.361>And let him find it. Trifles light as air</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.362>Are to the jealous confirmations strong</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.363>As proofs of holy writ: this may do something.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.364>The Moor already changes with my poison:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.365>Dangerous conceits are, in their natures, poisons.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.366>Which at the first are scarce found to distaste,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.367>But with a little act upon the blood.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.368>Burn like the mines of Sulphur. I did say so:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.369>Look, where he comes!</p>
<p><i>Re-enter OTHELLO</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.370>Not poppy, nor mandragora,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.371>Nor all the drowsy syrups of the world,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.372>Shall ever medicine thee to that sweet sleep</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.373>Which thou owedst yesterday.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech120><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.374>Ha! ha! false to me?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech121><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.375>Why, how now, general! no more of that.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech122><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.376>Avaunt! be gone! thou hast set me on the rack:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.377>I swear 'tis better to be much abused</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.378>Than but to know't a little.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech123><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.379>How now, my lord!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech124><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.380>What sense had I of her stol'n hours of lust?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.381>I saw't not, thought it not, it harm'd not me:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.382>I slept the next night well, was free and merry;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.383>I found not Cassio's kisses on her lips:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.384>He that is robb'd, not wanting what is stol'n,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.385>Let him not know't, and he's not robb'd at all.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech125><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.386>I am sorry to hear this.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech126><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.387>I had been happy, if the general camp,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.388>Pioners and all, had tasted her sweet body,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.389>So I had nothing known. O, now, for ever</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.390>Farewell the tranquil mind! farewell content!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.391>Farewell the plumed troop, and the big wars,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.392>That make ambition virtue! O, farewell!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.393>Farewell the neighing steed, and the shrill trump,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.394>The spirit-stirring drum, the ear-piercing fife,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.395>The royal banner, and all quality,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.396>Pride, pomp and circumstance of glorious war!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.397>And, O you mortal engines, whose rude throats</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.398>The immortal Jove's dead clamours counterfeit,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.399>Farewell! Othello's occupation's gone!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech127><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.400>Is't possible, my lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech128><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.401>Villain, be sure thou prove my love a whore,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.402>Be sure of it; give me the ocular proof:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.403>Or by the worth of man's eternal soul,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.404>Thou hadst been better have been born a dog</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.405>Than answer my waked wrath!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech129><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.406>Is't come to this?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech130><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.407>Make me to see't; or, at the least, so prove it,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.408>That the probation bear no hinge nor loop</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.409>To hang a doubt on; or woe upon thy life!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech131><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.410>My noble lord,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech132><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.411>If thou dost slander her and torture me,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.412>Never pray more; abandon all remorse;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.413>On horror's head horrors accumulate;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.414>Do deeds to make heaven weep, all earth amazed;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.415>For nothing canst thou to damnation add</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.416>Greater than that.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech133><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.417>                  O grace! O heaven forgive me!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.418>Are you a man? have you a soul or sense?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.419>God be wi' you; take mine office. O wretched fool.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.420>That livest to make thine honesty a vice!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.421>O monstrous world! Take note, take note, O world,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.422>To be direct and honest is not safe.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.423>I thank you for this profit; and from hence</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.424>I'll love no friend, sith love breeds such offence.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech134><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.425>Nay, stay: thou shouldst be honest.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech135><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.426>I should be wise, for honesty's a fool</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.427>And loses that it works for.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech136><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.428>By the world,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.429>I think my wife be honest and think she is not;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.430>I think that thou art just and think thou art not.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.431>I'll have some proof. Her name, that was as fresh</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.432>As Dian's visage, is now begrimed and black</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.433>As mine own face. If there be cords, or knives,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.434>Poison, or fire, or suffocating streams,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.435>I'll not endure it. Would I were satisfied!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech137><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.436>I see, sir, you are eaten up with passion:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.437>I do repent me that I put it to you.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.438>You would be satisfied?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech138><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.439>Would! nay, I will.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech139><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.440>And may: but, how? how satisfied, my lord?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.441>Would you, the supervisor, grossly gape on--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.442>Behold her topp'd?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech140><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.443>                  Death and damnation! O!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech141><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.444>It were a tedious difficulty, I think,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.445>To bring them to that prospect: damn them then,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.446>If ever mortal eyes do see them bolster</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.447>More than their own! What then? how then?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.448>What shall I say? Where's satisfaction?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.449>It is impossible you should see this,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.450>Were they as prime as goats, as hot as monkeys,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.451>As salt as wolves in pride, and fools as gross</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.452>As ignorance made drunk. But yet, I say,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.453>If imputation and strong circumstances,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.454>Which lead directly to the door of truth,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.455>Will give you satisfaction, you may have't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech142><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.456>Give me a living reason she's disloyal.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech143><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.457>I do not like the office:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.458>But, sith I am enter'd in this cause so far,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.459>Prick'd to't by foolish honesty and love,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.460>I will go on. I lay with Cassio lately;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.461>And, being troubled with a raging tooth,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.462>I could not sleep.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.463>There are a kind of men so loose of soul,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.464>That in their sleeps will mutter their affairs:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.465>One of this kind is Cassio:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.466>In sleep I heard him say 'Sweet Desdemona,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.467>Let us be wary, let us hide our loves;'</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.468>And then, sir, would he gripe and wring my hand,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.469>Cry 'O sweet creature!' and then kiss me hard,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.470>As if he pluck'd up kisses by the roots</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.471>That grew upon my lips: then laid his leg</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.472>Over my thigh, and sigh'd, and kiss'd; and then</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.473>Cried 'Cursed fate that gave thee to the Moor!'</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech144><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.474>O monstrous! monstrous!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech145><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.475>Nay, this was but his dream.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech146><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.476>But this denoted a foregone conclusion:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.477>'Tis a shrewd doubt, though it be but a dream.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech147><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.478>And this may help to thicken other proofs</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.479>That do demonstrate thinly.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech148><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.480>I'll tear her all to pieces.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech149><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.481>Nay, but be wise: yet we see nothing done;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.482>She may be honest yet. Tell me but this,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.483>Have you not sometimes seen a handkerchief</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.484>Spotted with strawberries in your wife's hand?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech150><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.485>I gave her such a one; 'twas my first gift.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech151><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.486>I know not that; but such a handkerchief--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.487>I am sure it was your wife's--did I to-day</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.488>See Cassio wipe his beard with.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech152><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.489>If it be that--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech153><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.490>If it be that, or any that was hers,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.491>It speaks against her with the other proofs.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech154><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.492>O, that the slave had forty thousand lives!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.493>One is too poor, too weak for my revenge.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.494>Now do I see 'tis true. Look here, Iago;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.495>All my fond love thus do I blow to heaven.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.496>'Tis gone.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.497>Arise, black vengeance, from thy hollow cell!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.498>Yield up, O love, thy crown and hearted throne</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.499>To tyrannous hate! Swell, bosom, with thy fraught,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.500>For 'tis of aspics' tongues!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech155><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.501>Yet be content.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech156><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.502>O, blood, blood, blood!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech157><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.503>Patience, I say; your mind perhaps may change.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech158><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.504>Never, Iago: Like to the Pontic sea,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.505>Whose icy current and compulsive course</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.506>Ne'er feels retiring ebb, but keeps due on</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.507>To the Propontic and the Hellespont,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.508>Even so my bloody thoughts, with violent pace,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.509>Shall ne'er look back, ne'er ebb to humble love,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.510>Till that a capable and wide revenge</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.511>Swallow them up. Now, by yond marble heaven,</p>
<p><i>Kneels</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.512>In the due reverence of a sacred vow</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.513>I here engage my words.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech159><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.514>Do not rise yet.</p>
<p><i>Kneels</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.515>Witness, you ever-burning lights above,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.516>You elements that clip us round about,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.517>Witness that here Iago doth give up</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.518>The execution of his wit, hands, heart,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.519>To wrong'd Othello's service! Let him command,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.520>And to obey shall be in me remorse,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.521>What bloody business ever.</p>
<p><i>They rise</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech160><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.522>I greet thy love,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.523>Not with vain thanks, but with acceptance bounteous,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.524>And will upon the instant put thee to't:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.525>Within these three days let me hear thee say</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.526>That Cassio's not alive.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech161><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.527>My friend is dead; 'tis done at your request:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.528>But let her live.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech162><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.529>Damn her, lewd minx! O, damn her!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.530>Come, go with me apart; I will withdraw,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.531>To furnish me with some swift means of death</p>
<p class="line" name=3.3.532>For the fair devil. Now art thou my lieutenant.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech163><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.3.533>I am your own for ever.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt</i></p>
</blockquote>
<h3>SCENE IV. Before the castle.</h3>
<p><blockquote>
<i>Enter DESDEMONA, EMILIA, and Clown</i>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech1><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.1>Do you know, sirrah, where Lieutenant Cassio lies?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech2><b>Clown</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.2>I dare not say he lies any where.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech3><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.3>Why, man?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech4><b>Clown</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.4>He's a soldier, and for one to say a soldier lies,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.5>is stabbing.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech5><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.6>Go to: where lodges he?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech6><b>Clown</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.7>To tell you where he lodges, is to tell you where I lie.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech7><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.8>Can any thing be made of this?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech8><b>Clown</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.9>I know not where he lodges, and for me to devise a</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.10>lodging and say he lies here or he lies there, were</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.11>to lie in mine own throat.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech9><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.12>Can you inquire him out, and be edified by report?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech10><b>Clown</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.13>I will catechise the world for him; that is, make</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.14>questions, and by them answer.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech11><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.15>Seek him, bid him come hither: tell him I have</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.16>moved my lord on his behalf, and hope all will be well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech12><b>Clown</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.17>To do this is within the compass of man's wit: and</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.18>therefore I will attempt the doing it.</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech13><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.19>Where should I lose that handkerchief, Emilia?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech14><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.20>I know not, madam.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech15><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.21>Believe me, I had rather have lost my purse</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.22>Full of crusadoes: and, but my noble Moor</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.23>Is true of mind and made of no such baseness</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.24>As jealous creatures are, it were enough</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.25>To put him to ill thinking.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech16><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.26>Is he not jealous?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech17><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.27>Who, he? I think the sun where he was born</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.28>Drew all such humours from him.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech18><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.29>Look, where he comes.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech19><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.30>I will not leave him now till Cassio</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.31>Be call'd to him.</p>
<p><i>Enter OTHELLO</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.32>How is't with you, my lord</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech20><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.33>Well, my good lady.</p>
<p><i>Aside</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.34>O, hardness to dissemble!--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.35>How do you, Desdemona?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech21><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.36>Well, my good lord.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech22><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.37>Give me your hand: this hand is moist, my lady.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech23><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.38>It yet hath felt no age nor known no sorrow.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech24><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.39>This argues fruitfulness and liberal heart:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.40>Hot, hot, and moist: this hand of yours requires</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.41>A sequester from liberty, fasting and prayer,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.42>Much castigation, exercise devout;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.43>For here's a young and sweating devil here,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.44>That commonly rebels. 'Tis a good hand,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.45>A frank one.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech25><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.46>                  You may, indeed, say so;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.47>For 'twas that hand that gave away my heart.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech26><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.48>A liberal hand: the hearts of old gave hands;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.49>But our new heraldry is hands, not hearts.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech27><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.50>I cannot speak of this. Come now, your promise.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech28><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.51>What promise, chuck?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech29><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.52>I have sent to bid Cassio come speak with you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech30><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.53>I have a salt and sorry rheum offends me;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.54>Lend me thy handkerchief.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech31><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.55>Here, my lord.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech32><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.56>That which I gave you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech33><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.57>I have it not about me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech34><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.58>Not?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech35><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.59>   No, indeed, my lord.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech36><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.60>That is a fault.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.61>That handkerchief</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.62>Did an Egyptian to my mother give;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.63>She was a charmer, and could almost read</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.64>The thoughts of people: she told her, while</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.65>she kept it,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.66>'Twould make her amiable and subdue my father</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.67>Entirely to her love, but if she lost it</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.68>Or made gift of it, my father's eye</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.69>Should hold her loathed and his spirits should hunt</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.70>After new fancies: she, dying, gave it me;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.71>And bid me, when my fate would have me wive,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.72>To give it her. I did so: and take heed on't;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.73>Make it a darling like your precious eye;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.74>To lose't or give't away were such perdition</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.75>As nothing else could match.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech37><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.76>Is't possible?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech38><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.77>'Tis true: there's magic in the web of it:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.78>A sibyl, that had number'd in the world</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.79>The sun to course two hundred compasses,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.80>In her prophetic fury sew'd the work;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.81>The worms were hallow'd that did breed the silk;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.82>And it was dyed in mummy which the skilful</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.83>Conserved of maidens' hearts.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech39><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.84>Indeed! is't true?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech40><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.85>Most veritable; therefore look to't well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech41><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.86>Then would to God that I had never seen't!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech42><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.87>Ha! wherefore?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech43><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.88>Why do you speak so startingly and rash?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech44><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.89>Is't lost? is't gone? speak, is it out</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.90>o' the way?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech45><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.91>Heaven bless us!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech46><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.92>Say you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech47><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.93>It is not lost; but what an if it were?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech48><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.94>How!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech49><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.95>I say, it is not lost.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech50><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.96>Fetch't, let me see't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech51><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.97>Why, so I can, sir, but I will not now.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.98>This is a trick to put me from my suit:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.99>Pray you, let Cassio be received again.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech52><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.100>Fetch me the handkerchief: my mind misgives.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech53><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.101>Come, come;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.102>You'll never meet a more sufficient man.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech54><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.103>The handkerchief!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech55><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.104>                  I pray, talk me of Cassio.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech56><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.105>The handkerchief!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech57><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.106>                  A man that all his time</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.107>Hath founded his good fortunes on your love,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.108>Shared dangers with you,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech58><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.109>The handkerchief!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech59><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.110>In sooth, you are to blame.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech60><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.111>Away!</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech61><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.112>Is not this man jealous?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech62><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.113>I ne'er saw this before.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.114>Sure, there's some wonder in this handkerchief:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.115>I am most unhappy in the loss of it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech63><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.116>'Tis not a year or two shows us a man:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.117>They are all but stomachs, and we all but food;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.118>To eat us hungerly, and when they are full,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.119>They belch us. Look you, Cassio and my husband!</p>
<p><i>Enter CASSIO and IAGO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech64><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.120>There is no other way; 'tis she must do't:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.121>And, lo, the happiness! go, and importune her.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech65><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.122>How now, good Cassio! what's the news with you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech66><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.123>Madam, my former suit: I do beseech you</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.124>That by your virtuous means I may again</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.125>Exist, and be a member of his love</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.126>Whom I with all the office of my heart</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.127>Entirely honour: I would not be delay'd.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.128>If my offence be of such mortal kind</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.129>That nor my service past, nor present sorrows,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.130>Nor purposed merit in futurity,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.131>Can ransom me into his love again,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.132>But to know so must be my benefit;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.133>So shall I clothe me in a forced content,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.134>And shut myself up in some other course,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.135>To fortune's alms.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech67><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.136>                  Alas, thrice-gentle Cassio!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.137>My advocation is not now in tune;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.138>My lord is not my lord; nor should I know him,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.139>Were he in favour as in humour alter'd.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.140>So help me every spirit sanctified,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.141>As I have spoken for you all my best</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.142>And stood within the blank of his displeasure</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.143>For my free speech! you must awhile be patient:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.144>What I can do I will; and more I will</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.145>Than for myself I dare: let that suffice you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech68><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.146>Is my lord angry?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech69><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.147>                  He went hence but now,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.148>And certainly in strange unquietness.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech70><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.149>Can he be angry? I have seen the cannon,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.150>When it hath blown his ranks into the air,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.151>And, like the devil, from his very arm</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.152>Puff'd his own brother:--and can he be angry?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.153>Something of moment then: I will go meet him:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.154>There's matter in't indeed, if he be angry.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech71><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.155>I prithee, do so.</p>
<p><i>Exit IAGO</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.156>Something, sure, of state,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.157>Either from Venice, or some unhatch'd practise</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.158>Made demonstrable here in Cyprus to him,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.159>Hath puddled his clear spirit: and in such cases</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.160>Men's natures wrangle with inferior things,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.161>Though great ones are their object. 'Tis even so;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.162>For let our finger ache, and it indues</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.163>Our other healthful members even to that sense</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.164>Of pain: nay, we must think men are not gods,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.165>Nor of them look for such observances</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.166>As fit the bridal. Beshrew me much, Emilia,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.167>I was, unhandsome warrior as I am,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.168>Arraigning his unkindness with my soul;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.169>But now I find I had suborn'd the witness,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.170>And he's indicted falsely.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech72><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.171>Pray heaven it be state-matters, as you think,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.172>And no conception nor no jealous toy</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.173>Concerning you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech73><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.174>Alas the day! I never gave him cause.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech74><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.175>But jealous souls will not be answer'd so;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.176>They are not ever jealous for the cause,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.177>But jealous for they are jealous: 'tis a monster</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.178>Begot upon itself, born on itself.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech75><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.179>Heaven keep that monster from Othello's mind!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech76><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.180>Lady, amen.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech77><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.181>I will go seek him. Cassio, walk hereabout:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.182>If I do find him fit, I'll move your suit</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.183>And seek to effect it to my uttermost.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech78><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.184>I humbly thank your ladyship.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt DESDEMONA and EMILIA</i></p>
<p><i>Enter BIANCA</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech79><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.185>Save you, friend Cassio!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech80><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.186>What make you from home?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.187>How is it with you, my most fair Bianca?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.188>I' faith, sweet love, I was coming to your house.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech81><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.189>And I was going to your lodging, Cassio.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.190>What, keep a week away? seven days and nights?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.191>Eight score eight hours? and lovers' absent hours,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.192>More tedious than the dial eight score times?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.193>O weary reckoning!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech82><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.194>                  Pardon me, Bianca:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.195>I have this while with leaden thoughts been press'd:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.196>But I shall, in a more continuate time,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.197>Strike off this score of absence. Sweet Bianca,</p>
<p><i>Giving her DESDEMONA's handkerchief</i></p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.198>Take me this work out.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech83><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.199>O Cassio, whence came this?</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.200>This is some token from a newer friend:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.201>To the felt absence now I feel a cause:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.202>Is't come to this? Well, well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech84><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.203>Go to, woman!</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.204>Throw your vile guesses in the devil's teeth,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.205>From whence you have them. You are jealous now</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.206>That this is from some mistress, some remembrance:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.207>No, in good troth, Bianca.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech85><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.208>Why, whose is it?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech86><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.209>I know not, sweet: I found it in my chamber.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.210>I like the work well: ere it be demanded--</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.211>As like enough it will--I'ld have it copied:</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.212>Take it, and do't; and leave me for this time.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech87><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.213>Leave you! wherefore?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech88><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.214>I do attend here on the general;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.215>And think it no addition, nor my wish,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.216>To have him see me woman'd.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech89><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.217>Why, I pray you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech90><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.218>Not that I love you not.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech91><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.219>But that you do not love me.</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.220>I pray you, bring me on the way a little,</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.221>And say if I shall see you soon at night.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech92><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.222>'Tis but a little way that I can bring you;</p>
<p class="line" name=3.4.223>For I attend here: but I'll see you soon.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech93><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=3.4.224>'Tis very good; I must be circumstanced.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt</i></p>
</blockquote><p>
<H3>ACT IV</h3>
<h3>SCENE I. Cyprus. Before the castle.</h3>
<p><blockquote>
<i>Enter OTHELLO and IAGO</i>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech1><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.1>Will you think so?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech2><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.2>                  Think so, Iago!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech3><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.3>What,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.4>To kiss in private?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech4><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.5>An unauthorized kiss.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech5><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.6>Or to be naked with her friend in bed</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.7>An hour or more, not meaning any harm?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech6><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.8>Naked in bed, Iago, and not mean harm!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.9>It is hypocrisy against the devil:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.10>They that mean virtuously, and yet do so,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.11>The devil their virtue tempts, and they tempt heaven.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech7><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.12>So they do nothing, 'tis a venial slip:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.13>But if I give my wife a handkerchief,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech8><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.14>What then?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech9><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.15>Why, then, 'tis hers, my lord; and, being hers,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.16>She may, I think, bestow't on any man.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech10><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.17>She is protectress of her honour too:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.18>May she give that?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech11><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.19>Her honour is an essence that's not seen;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.20>They have it very oft that have it not:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.21>But, for the handkerchief,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech12><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.22>By heaven, I would most gladly have forgot it.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.23>Thou said'st, it comes o'er my memory,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.24>As doth the raven o'er the infected house,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.25>Boding to all--he had my handkerchief.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech13><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.26>Ay, what of that?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech14><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.27>                  That's not so good now.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech15><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.28>What,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.29>If I had said I had seen him do you wrong?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.30>Or heard him say,--as knaves be such abroad,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.31>Who having, by their own importunate suit,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.32>Or voluntary dotage of some mistress,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.33>Convinced or supplied them, cannot choose</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.34>But they must blab--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech16><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.35>Hath he said any thing?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech17><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.36>He hath, my lord; but be you well assured,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.37>No more than he'll unswear.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech18><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.38>What hath he said?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech19><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.39>'Faith, that he did--I know not what he did.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech20><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.40>What? what?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech21><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.41>Lie--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech22><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.42>    With her?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech23><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.43>With her, on her; what you will.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech24><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.44>Lie with her! lie on her! We say lie on her, when</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.45>they belie her. Lie with her! that's fulsome.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.46>--Handkerchief--confessions--handkerchief!--To</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.47>confess, and be hanged for his labour;--first, to be</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.48>hanged, and then to confess.--I tremble at it.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.49>Nature would not invest herself in such shadowing</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.50>passion without some instruction. It is not words</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.51>that shake me thus. Pish! Noses, ears, and lips.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.52>--Is't possible?--Confess--handkerchief!--O devil!--</p>
<p><i>Falls in a trance</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech25><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.53>Work on,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.54>My medicine, work! Thus credulous fools are caught;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.55>And many worthy and chaste dames even thus,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.56>All guiltless, meet reproach. What, ho! my lord!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.57>My lord, I say! Othello!</p>
<p><i>Enter CASSIO</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.58>How now, Cassio!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech26><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.59>What's the matter?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech27><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.60>My lord is fall'n into an epilepsy:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.61>This is his second fit; he had one yesterday.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech28><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.62>Rub him about the temples.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech29><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.63>No, forbear;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.64>The lethargy must have his quiet course:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.65>If not, he foams at mouth and by and by</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.66>Breaks out to savage madness. Look he stirs:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.67>Do you withdraw yourself a little while,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.68>He will recover straight: when he is gone,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.69>I would on great occasion speak with you.</p>
<p><i>Exit CASSIO</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.70>How is it, general? have you not hurt your head?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech30><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.71>Dost thou mock me?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech31><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.72>                  I mock you! no, by heaven.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.73>Would you would bear your fortune like a man!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech32><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.74>A horned man's a monster and a beast.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech33><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.75>There's many a beast then in a populous city,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.76>And many a civil monster.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech34><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.77>Did he confess it?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech35><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.78>                  Good sir, be a man;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.79>Think every bearded fellow that's but yoked</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.80>May draw with you: there's millions now alive</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.81>That nightly lie in those unproper beds</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.82>Which they dare swear peculiar: your case is better.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.83>O, 'tis the spite of hell, the fiend's arch-mock,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.84>To lip a wanton in a secure couch,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.85>And to suppose her chaste! No, let me know;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.86>And knowing what I am, I know what she shall be.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech36><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.87>O, thou art wise; 'tis certain.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech37><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.88>Stand you awhile apart;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.89>Confine yourself but in a patient list.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.90>Whilst you were here o'erwhelmed with your grief--</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.91>A passion most unsuiting such a man--</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.92>Cassio came hither: I shifted him away,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.93>And laid good 'scuse upon your ecstasy,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.94>Bade him anon return and here speak with me;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.95>The which he promised. Do but encave yourself,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.96>And mark the fleers, the gibes, and notable scorns,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.97>That dwell in every region of his face;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.98>For I will make him tell the tale anew,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.99>Where, how, how oft, how long ago, and when</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.100>He hath, and is again to cope your wife:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.101>I say, but mark his gesture. Marry, patience;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.102>Or I shall say you are all in all in spleen,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.103>And nothing of a man.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech38><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.104>Dost thou hear, Iago?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.105>I will be found most cunning in my patience;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.106>But--dost thou hear?--most bloody.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech39><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.107>That's not amiss;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.108>But yet keep time in all. Will you withdraw?</p>
<p><i>OTHELLO retires</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.109>Now will I question Cassio of Bianca,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.110>A housewife that by selling her desires</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.111>Buys herself bread and clothes: it is a creature</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.112>That dotes on Cassio; as 'tis the strumpet's plague</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.113>To beguile many and be beguiled by one:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.114>He, when he hears of her, cannot refrain</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.115>From the excess of laughter. Here he comes:</p>
<p><i>Re-enter CASSIO</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.116>As he shall smile, Othello shall go mad;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.117>And his unbookish jealousy must construe</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.118>Poor Cassio's smiles, gestures and light behavior,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.119>Quite in the wrong. How do you now, lieutenant?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech40><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.120>The worser that you give me the addition</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.121>Whose want even kills me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech41><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.122>Ply Desdemona well, and you are sure on't.</p>
<p><i>Speaking lower</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.123>Now, if this suit lay in Bianco's power,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.124>How quickly should you speed!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech42><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.125>Alas, poor caitiff!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech43><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.126>Look, how he laughs already!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech44><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.127>I never knew woman love man so.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech45><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.128>Alas, poor rogue! I think, i' faith, she loves me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech46><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.129>Now he denies it faintly, and laughs it out.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech47><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.130>Do you hear, Cassio?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech48><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.131>Now he importunes him</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.132>To tell it o'er: go to; well said, well said.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech49><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.133>She gives it out that you shall marry hey:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.134>Do you intend it?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech50><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.135>Ha, ha, ha!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech51><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.136>Do you triumph, Roman? do you triumph?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech52><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.137>I marry her! what? a customer! Prithee, bear some</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.138>charity to my wit: do not think it so unwholesome.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.139>Ha, ha, ha!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech53><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.140>So, so, so, so: they laugh that win.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech54><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.141>'Faith, the cry goes that you shall marry her.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech55><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.142>Prithee, say true.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech56><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.143>I am a very villain else.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech57><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.144>Have you scored me? Well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech58><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.145>This is the monkey's own giving out: she is</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.146>persuaded I will marry her, out of her own love and</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.147>flattery, not out of my promise.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech59><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.148>Iago beckons me; now he begins the story.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech60><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.149>She was here even now; she haunts me in every place.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.150>I was the other day talking on the sea-bank with</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.151>certain Venetians; and thither comes the bauble,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.152>and, by this hand, she falls me thus about my neck--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech61><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.153>Crying 'O dear Cassio!' as it were: his gesture</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.154>imports it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech62><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.155>So hangs, and lolls, and weeps upon me; so hales,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.156>and pulls me: ha, ha, ha!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech63><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.157>Now he tells how she plucked him to my chamber. O,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.158>I see that nose of yours, but not that dog I shall</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.159>throw it to.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech64><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.160>Well, I must leave her company.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech65><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.161>Before me! look, where she comes.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech66><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.162>'Tis such another fitchew! marry a perfumed one.</p>
<p><i>Enter BIANCA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.163>What do you mean by this haunting of me?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech67><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.164>Let the devil and his dam haunt you! What did you</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.165>mean by that same handkerchief you gave me even now?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.166>I was a fine fool to take it. I must take out the</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.167>work?--A likely piece of work, that you should find</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.168>it in your chamber, and not know who left it there!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.169>This is some minx's token, and I must take out the</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.170>work? There; give it your hobby-horse: wheresoever</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.171>you had it, I'll take out no work on't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech68><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.172>How now, my sweet Bianca! how now! how now!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech69><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.173>By heaven, that should be my handkerchief!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech70><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.174>An you'll come to supper to-night, you may; an you</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.175>will not, come when you are next prepared for.</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech71><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.176>After her, after her.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech72><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.177>'Faith, I must; she'll rail in the street else.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech73><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.178>Will you sup there?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech74><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.179>'Faith, I intend so.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech75><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.180>Well, I may chance to see you; for I would very fain</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.181>speak with you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech76><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.182>Prithee, come; will you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech77><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.183>Go to; say no more.</p>
<p><i>Exit CASSIO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech78><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.184>[Advancing]  How shall I murder him, Iago?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech79><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.185>Did you perceive how he laughed at his vice?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech80><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.186>O Iago!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech81><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.187>And did you see the handkerchief?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech82><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.188>Was that mine?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech83><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.189>Yours by this hand: and to see how he prizes the</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.190>foolish woman your wife! she gave it him, and he</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.191>hath given it his whore.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech84><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.192>I would have him nine years a-killing.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.193>A fine woman! a fair woman! a sweet woman!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech85><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.194>Nay, you must forget that.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech86><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.195>Ay, let her rot, and perish, and be damned to-night;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.196>for she shall not live: no, my heart is turned to</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.197>stone; I strike it, and it hurts my hand. O, the</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.198>world hath not a sweeter creature: she might lie by</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.199>an emperor's side and command him tasks.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech87><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.200>Nay, that's not your way.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech88><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.201>Hang her! I do but say what she is: so delicate</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.202>with her needle: an admirable musician: O! she</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.203>will sing the savageness out of a bear: of so high</p>
