<p class="line" name=4.1.204>and plenteous wit and invention:--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech89><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.205>She's the worse for all this.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech90><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.206>O, a thousand thousand times: and then, of so</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.207>gentle a condition!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech91><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.208>Ay, too gentle.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech92><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.209>Nay, that's certain: but yet the pity of it, Iago!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.210>O Iago, the pity of it, Iago!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech93><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.211>If you are so fond over her iniquity, give her</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.212>patent to offend; for, if it touch not you, it comes</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.213>near nobody.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech94><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.214>I will chop her into messes: cuckold me!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech95><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.215>O, 'tis foul in her.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech96><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.216>With mine officer!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech97><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.217>That's fouler.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech98><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.218>Get me some poison, Iago; this night: I'll not</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.219>expostulate with her, lest her body and beauty</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.220>unprovide my mind again: this night, Iago.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech99><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.221>Do it not with poison, strangle her in her bed, even</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.222>the bed she hath contaminated.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech100><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.223>Good, good: the justice of it pleases: very good.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech101><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.224>And for Cassio, let me be his undertaker: you</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.225>shall hear more by midnight.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech102><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.226>Excellent good.</p>
<p><i>A trumpet within</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.227>What trumpet is that same?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech103><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.228>Something from Venice, sure. 'Tis Lodovico</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.229>Come from the duke: and, see, your wife is with him.</p>
<p><i>Enter LODOVICO, DESDEMONA, and Attendants</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech104><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.230>Save you, worthy general!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech105><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.231>With all my heart, sir.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech106><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.232>The duke and senators of Venice greet you.</p>
<p><i>Gives him a letter</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech107><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.233>I kiss the instrument of their pleasures.</p>
<p><i>Opens the letter, and reads</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech108><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.234>And what's the news, good cousin Lodovico?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech109><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.235>I am very glad to see you, signior</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.236>Welcome to Cyprus.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech110><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.237>I thank you. How does Lieutenant Cassio?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech111><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.238>Lives, sir.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech112><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.239>Cousin, there's fall'n between him and my lord</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.240>An unkind breach: but you shall make all well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech113><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.241>Are you sure of that?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech114><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.242>My lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech115><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.243>[Reads]  'This fail you not to do, as you will--'</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech116><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.244>He did not call; he's busy in the paper.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.245>Is there division 'twixt my lord and Cassio?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech117><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.246>A most unhappy one: I would do much</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.247>To atone them, for the love I bear to Cassio.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech118><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.248>Fire and brimstone!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech119><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.249>My lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech120><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.250>       Are you wise?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech121><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.251>What, is he angry?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech122><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.252>                  May be the letter moved him;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.253>For, as I think, they do command him home,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.254>Deputing Cassio in his government.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech123><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.255>Trust me, I am glad on't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech124><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.256>Indeed!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech125><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.257>My lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech126><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.258>I am glad to see you mad.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech127><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.259>Why, sweet Othello,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech128><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.260>[Striking her]  Devil!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech129><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.261>I have not deserved this.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech130><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.262>My lord, this would not be believed in Venice,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.263>Though I should swear I saw't: 'tis very much:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.264>Make her amends; she weeps.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech131><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.265>O devil, devil!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.266>If that the earth could teem with woman's tears,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.267>Each drop she falls would prove a crocodile.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.268>Out of my sight!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech132><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.269>I will not stay to offend you.</p>
<p><i>Going</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech133><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.270>Truly, an obedient lady:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.271>I do beseech your lordship, call her back.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech134><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.272>Mistress!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech135><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.273>        My lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech136><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.274>What would you with her, sir?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech137><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.275>Who, I, my lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech138><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.276>Ay; you did wish that I would make her turn:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.277>Sir, she can turn, and turn, and yet go on,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.278>And turn again; and she can weep, sir, weep;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.279>And she's obedient, as you say, obedient,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.280>Very obedient. Proceed you in your tears.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.281>Concerning this, sir,--O  well-painted passion!--</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.282>I am commanded home. Get you away;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.283>I'll send for you anon. Sir, I obey the mandate,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.284>And will return to Venice. Hence, avaunt!</p>
<p><i>Exit DESDEMONA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.285>Cassio shall have my place. And, sir, tonight,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.286>I do entreat that we may sup together:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.287>You are welcome, sir, to Cyprus.--Goats and monkeys!</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech139><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.288>Is this the noble Moor whom our full senate</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.289>Call all in all sufficient? Is this the nature</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.290>Whom passion could not shake? whose solid virtue</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.291>The shot of accident, nor dart of chance,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.292>Could neither graze nor pierce?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech140><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.293>He is much changed.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech141><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.294>Are his wits safe? is he not light of brain?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech142><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.295>He's that he is: I may not breathe my censure</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.296>What he might be: if what he might he is not,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.297>I would to heaven he were!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech143><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.298>What, strike his wife!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech144><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.299>'Faith, that was not so well; yet would I knew</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.300>That stroke would prove the worst!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech145><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.301>Is it his use?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.302>Or did the letters work upon his blood,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.303>And new-create this fault?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech146><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.304>Alas, alas!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.305>It is not honesty in me to speak</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.306>What I have seen and known. You shall observe him,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.307>And his own courses will denote him so</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.308>That I may save my speech: do but go after,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.1.309>And mark how he continues.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech147><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.1.310>I am sorry that I am deceived in him.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt</i></p>
</blockquote>
<h3>SCENE II. A room in the castle.</h3>
<p><blockquote>
<i>Enter OTHELLO and EMILIA</i>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech1><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.1>You have seen nothing then?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech2><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.2>Nor ever heard, nor ever did suspect.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech3><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.3>Yes, you have seen Cassio and she together.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech4><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.4>But then I saw no harm, and then I heard</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.5>Each syllable that breath made up between them.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech5><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.6>What, did they never whisper?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech6><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.7>Never, my lord.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech7><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.8>Nor send you out o' the way?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech8><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.9>Never.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech9><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.10>To fetch her fan, her gloves, her mask, nor nothing?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech10><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.11>Never, my lord.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech11><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.12>That's strange.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech12><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.13>I durst, my lord, to wager she is honest,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.14>Lay down my soul at stake: if you think other,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.15>Remove your thought; it doth abuse your bosom.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.16>If any wretch have put this in your head,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.17>Let heaven requite it with the serpent's curse!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.18>For, if she be not honest, chaste, and true,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.19>There's no man happy; the purest of their wives</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.20>Is foul as slander.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech13><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.21>Bid her come hither: go.</p>
<p><i>Exit EMILIA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.22>She says enough; yet she's a simple bawd</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.23>That cannot say as much. This is a subtle whore,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.24>A closet lock and key of villanous secrets</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.25>And yet she'll kneel and pray; I have seen her do't.</p>
<p><i>Enter DESDEMONA with EMILIA</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech14><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.26>My lord, what is your will?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech15><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.27>Pray, chuck, come hither.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech16><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.28>What is your pleasure?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech17><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.29>Let me see your eyes;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.30>Look in my face.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech18><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.31>                  What horrible fancy's this?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech19><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.32>[To EMILIA]  Some of your function, mistress;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.33>Leave procreants alone and shut the door;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.34>Cough, or cry 'hem,' if any body come:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.35>Your mystery, your mystery: nay, dispatch.</p>
<p><i>Exit EMILIA</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech20><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.36>Upon my knees, what doth your speech import?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.37>I understand a fury in your words.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.38>But not the words.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech21><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.39>Why, what art thou?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech22><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.40>Your wife, my lord; your true</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.41>And loyal wife.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech23><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.42>                  Come, swear it, damn thyself</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.43>Lest, being like one of heaven, the devils themselves</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.44>Should fear to seize thee: therefore be double damn'd:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.45>Swear thou art honest.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech24><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.46>Heaven doth truly know it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech25><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.47>Heaven truly knows that thou art false as hell.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech26><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.48>To whom, my lord? with whom? how am I false?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech27><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.49>O Desdemona! away! away! away!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech28><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.50>Alas the heavy day! Why do you weep?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.51>Am I the motive of these tears, my lord?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.52>If haply you my father do suspect</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.53>An instrument of this your calling back,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.54>Lay not your blame on me: If you have lost him,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.55>Why, I have lost him too.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech29><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.56>Had it pleased heaven</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.57>To try me with affliction; had they rain'd</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.58>All kinds of sores and shames on my bare head.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.59>Steep'd me in poverty to the very lips,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.60>Given to captivity me and my utmost hopes,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.61>I should have found in some place of my soul</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.62>A drop of patience: but, alas, to make me</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.63>A fixed figure for the time of scorn</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.64>To point his slow unmoving finger at!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.65>Yet could I bear that too; well, very well:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.66>But there, where I have garner'd up my heart,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.67>Where either I must live, or bear no life;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.68>The fountain from the which my current runs,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.69>Or else dries up; to be discarded thence!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.70>Or keep it as a cistern for foul toads</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.71>To knot and gender in! Turn thy complexion there,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.72>Patience, thou young and rose-lipp'd cherubin,--</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.73>Ay, there, look grim as hell!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech30><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.74>I hope my noble lord esteems me honest.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech31><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.75>O, ay; as summer flies are in the shambles,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.76>That quicken even with blowing. O thou weed,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.77>Who art so lovely fair and smell'st so sweet</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.78>That the sense aches at thee, would thou hadst</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.79>ne'er been born!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech32><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.80>Alas, what ignorant sin have I committed?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech33><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.81>Was this fair paper, this most goodly book,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.82>Made to write 'whore' upon? What committed!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.83>Committed! O thou public commoner!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.84>I should make very forges of my cheeks,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.85>That would to cinders burn up modesty,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.86>Did I but speak thy deeds. What committed!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.87>Heaven stops the nose at it and the moon winks,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.88>The bawdy wind that kisses all it meets</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.89>Is hush'd within the hollow mine of earth,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.90>And will not hear it. What committed!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.91>Impudent strumpet!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech34><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.92>                  By heaven, you do me wrong.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech35><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.93>Are you not a strumpet?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech36><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.94>No, as I am a Christian:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.95>If to preserve this vessel for my lord</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.96>From any other foul unlawful touch</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.97>Be not to be a strumpet, I am none.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech37><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.98>What, not a whore?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech38><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.99>                  No, as I shall be saved.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech39><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.100>Is't possible?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech40><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.101>                  O, heaven forgive us!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech41><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.102>I cry you mercy, then:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.103>I took you for that cunning whore of Venice</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.104>That married with Othello.</p>
<p><i>Raising his voice</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.105>You, mistress,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.106>That have the office opposite to Saint Peter,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.107>And keep the gate of hell!</p>
<p><i>Re-enter EMILIA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.108>You, you, ay, you!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.109>We have done our course; there's money for your pains:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.110>I pray you, turn the key and keep our counsel.</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech42><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.111>Alas, what does this gentleman conceive?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.112>How do you, madam? how do you, my good lady?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech43><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.113>'Faith, half asleep.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech44><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.114>Good madam, what's the matter with my lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech45><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.115>With who?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech46><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.116>Why, with my lord, madam.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech47><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.117>Who is thy lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech48><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.118>                  He that is yours, sweet lady.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech49><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.119>I have none: do not talk to me, Emilia;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.120>I cannot weep; nor answer have I none,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.121>But what should go by water. Prithee, tonight</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.122>Lay on my bed my wedding sheets: remember;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.123>And call thy husband hither.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech50><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.124>Here's a change indeed!</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech51><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.125>'Tis meet I should be used so, very meet.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.126>How have I been behaved, that he might stick</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.127>The small'st opinion on my least misuse?</p>
<p><i>Re-enter EMILIA with IAGO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech52><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.128>What is your pleasure, madam?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.129>How is't with you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech53><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.130>I cannot tell. Those that do teach young babes</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.131>Do it with gentle means and easy tasks:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.132>He might have chid me so; for, in good faith,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.133>I am a child to chiding.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech54><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.134>What's the matter, lady?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech55><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.135>Alas, Iago, my lord hath so bewhored her.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.136>Thrown such despite and heavy terms upon her,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.137>As true hearts cannot bear.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech56><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.138>Am I that name, Iago?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech57><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.139>What name, fair lady?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech58><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.140>Such as she says my lord did say I was.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech59><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.141>He call'd her whore: a beggar in his drink</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.142>Could not have laid such terms upon his callat.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech60><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.143>Why did he so?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech61><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.144>I do not know; I am sure I am none such.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech62><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.145>Do not weep, do not weep. Alas the day!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech63><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.146>Hath she forsook so many noble matches,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.147>Her father and her country and her friends,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.148>To be call'd whore? would it not make one weep?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech64><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.149>It is my wretched fortune.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech65><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.150>Beshrew him for't!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.151>How comes this trick upon him?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech66><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.152>Nay, heaven doth know.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech67><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.153>I will be hang'd, if some eternal villain,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.154>Some busy and insinuating rogue,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.155>Some cogging, cozening slave, to get some office,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.156>Have not devised this slander; I'll be hang'd else.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech68><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.157>Fie, there is no such man; it is impossible.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech69><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.158>If any such there be, heaven pardon him!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech70><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.159>A halter pardon him! and hell gnaw his bones!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.160>Why should he call her whore? who keeps her company?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.161>What place? what time? what form? what likelihood?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.162>The Moor's abused by some most villanous knave,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.163>Some base notorious knave, some scurvy fellow.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.164>O heaven, that such companions thou'ldst unfold,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.165>And put in every honest hand a whip</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.166>To lash the rascals naked through the world</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.167>Even from the east to the west!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech71><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.168>Speak within door.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech72><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.169>O, fie upon them! Some such squire he was</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.170>That turn'd your wit the seamy side without,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.171>And made you to suspect me with the Moor.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech73><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.172>You are a fool; go to.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech74><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.173>O good Iago,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.174>What shall I do to win my lord again?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.175>Good friend, go to him; for, by this light of heaven,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.176>I know not how I lost him. Here I kneel:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.177>If e'er my will did trespass 'gainst his love,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.178>Either in discourse of thought or actual deed,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.179>Or that mine eyes, mine ears, or any sense,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.180>Delighted them in any other form;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.181>Or that I do not yet, and ever did.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.182>And ever will--though he do shake me off</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.183>To beggarly divorcement--love him dearly,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.184>Comfort forswear me! Unkindness may do much;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.185>And his unkindness may defeat my life,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.186>But never taint my love. I cannot say 'whore:'</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.187>It does abhor me now I speak the word;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.188>To do the act that might the addition earn</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.189>Not the world's mass of vanity could make me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech75><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.190>I pray you, be content; 'tis but his humour:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.191>The business of the state does him offence,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.192>And he does chide with you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech76><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.193>If 'twere no other--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech77><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.194>'Tis but so, I warrant.</p>
<p><i>Trumpets within</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.195>Hark, how these instruments summon to supper!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.196>The messengers of Venice stay the meat;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.197>Go in, and weep not; all things shall be well.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt DESDEMONA and EMILIA</i></p>
<p><i>Enter RODERIGO</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.198>How now, Roderigo!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech78><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.199>I do not find that thou dealest justly with me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech79><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.200>What in the contrary?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech80><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.201>Every day thou daffest me with some device, Iago;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.202>and rather, as it seems to me now, keepest from me</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.203>all conveniency than suppliest me with the least</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.204>advantage of hope. I will indeed no longer endure</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.205>it, nor am I yet persuaded to put up in peace what</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.206>already I have foolishly suffered.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech81><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.207>Will you hear me, Roderigo?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech82><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.208>'Faith, I have heard too much, for your words and</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.209>performances are no kin together.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech83><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.210>You charge me most unjustly.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech84><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.211>With nought but truth. I have wasted myself out of</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.212>my means. The jewels you have had from me to</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.213>deliver to Desdemona would half have corrupted a</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.214>votarist: you have told me she hath received them</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.215>and returned me expectations and comforts of sudden</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.216>respect and acquaintance, but I find none.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech85><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.217>Well; go to; very well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech86><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.218>Very well! go to! I cannot go to, man; nor 'tis</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.219>not very well: nay, I think it is scurvy, and begin</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.220>to find myself fobbed in it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech87><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.221>Very well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech88><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.222>I tell you 'tis not very well. I will make myself</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.223>known to Desdemona: if she will return me my</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.224>jewels, I will give over my suit and repent my</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.225>unlawful solicitation; if not, assure yourself I</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.226>will seek satisfaction of you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech89><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.227>You have said now.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech90><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.228>Ay, and said nothing but what I protest intendment of doing.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech91><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.229>Why, now I see there's mettle in thee, and even from</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.230>this instant to build on thee a better opinion than</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.231>ever before. Give me thy hand, Roderigo: thou hast</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.232>taken against me a most just exception; but yet, I</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.233>protest, I have dealt most directly in thy affair.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech92><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.234>It hath not appeared.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech93><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.235>I grant indeed it hath not appeared, and your</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.236>suspicion is not without wit and judgment. But,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.237>Roderigo, if thou hast that in thee indeed, which I</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.238>have greater reason to believe now than ever, I mean</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.239>purpose, courage and valour, this night show it: if</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.240>thou the next night following enjoy not Desdemona,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.241>take me from this world with treachery and devise</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.242>engines for my life.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech94><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.243>Well, what is it? is it within reason and compass?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech95><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.244>Sir, there is especial commission come from Venice</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.245>to depute Cassio in Othello's place.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech96><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.246>Is that true? why, then Othello and Desdemona</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.247>return again to Venice.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech97><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.248>O, no; he goes into Mauritania and takes away with</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.249>him the fair Desdemona, unless his abode be</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.250>lingered here by some accident: wherein none can be</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.251>so determinate as the removing of Cassio.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech98><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.252>How do you mean, removing of him?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech99><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.253>Why, by making him uncapable of Othello's place;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.254>knocking out his brains.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech100><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.255>And that you would have me to do?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech101><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.256>Ay, if you dare do yourself a profit and a right.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.257>He sups to-night with a harlotry, and thither will I</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.258>go to him: he knows not yet of his horrorable</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.259>fortune. If you will watch his going thence, which</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.260>I will fashion to fall out between twelve and one,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.261>you may take him at your pleasure: I will be near</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.262>to second your attempt, and he shall fall between</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.263>us. Come, stand not amazed at it, but go along with</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.264>me; I will show you such a necessity in his death</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.265>that you shall think yourself bound to put it on</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.266>him. It is now high suppertime, and the night grows</p>
<p class="line" name=4.2.267>to waste: about it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech102><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.268>I will hear further reason for this.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech103><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.2.269>And you shall be satisfied.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt</i></p>
</blockquote>
<h3>SCENE III. Another room In the castle.</h3>
<p><blockquote>
<i>Enter OTHELLO, LODOVICO, DESDEMONA, EMILIA and Attendants</i>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech1><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.1>I do beseech you, sir, trouble yourself no further.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech2><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.2>O, pardon me: 'twill do me good to walk.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech3><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.3>Madam, good night; I humbly thank your ladyship.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech4><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.4>Your honour is most welcome.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech5><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.5>Will you walk, sir?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.6>O,--Desdemona,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech6><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.7>My lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech7><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.8>Get you to bed on the instant; I will be returned</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.9>forthwith: dismiss your attendant there: look it be done.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech8><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.10>I will, my lord.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt OTHELLO, LODOVICO, and Attendants</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech9><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.11>How goes it now? he looks gentler than he did.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech10><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.12>He says he will return incontinent:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.13>He hath commanded me to go to bed,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.14>And bade me to dismiss you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech11><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.15>Dismiss me!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech12><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.16>It was his bidding: therefore, good Emilia,.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.17>Give me my nightly wearing, and adieu:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.18>We must not now displease him.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech13><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.19>I would you had never seen him!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech14><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.20>So would not I	my love doth so approve him,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.21>That even his stubbornness, his cheques, his frowns--</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.22>Prithee, unpin me,--have grace and favour in them.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech15><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.23>I have laid those sheets you bade me on the bed.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech16><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.24>All's one. Good faith, how foolish are our minds!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.25>If I do die before thee prithee, shroud me</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.26>In one of those same sheets.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech17><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.27>Come, come you talk.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech18><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.28>My mother had a maid call'd Barbara:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.29>She was in love, and he she loved proved mad</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.30>And did forsake her: she had a song of 'willow;'</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.31>An old thing 'twas, but it express'd her fortune,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.32>And she died singing it: that song to-night</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.33>Will not go from my mind; I have much to do,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.34>But to go hang my head all at one side,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.35>And sing it like poor Barbara. Prithee, dispatch.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech19><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.36>Shall I go fetch your night-gown?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech20><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.37>No, unpin me here.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.38>This Lodovico is a proper man.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech21><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.39>A very handsome man.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech22><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.40>He speaks well.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech23><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.41>I know a lady in Venice would have walked barefoot</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.42>to Palestine for a touch of his nether lip.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech24><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.43>[Singing]  The poor soul sat sighing by a sycamore tree,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.44>Sing all a green willow:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.45>Her hand on her bosom, her head on her knee,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.46>Sing willow, willow, willow:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.47>The fresh streams ran by her, and murmur'd her moans;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.48>Sing willow, willow, willow;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.49>Her salt tears fell from her, and soften'd the stones;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.50>Lay by these:--</p>
<p><i>Singing</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.51>Sing willow, willow, willow;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.52>Prithee, hie thee; he'll come anon:--</p>
<p><i>Singing</i></p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.53>Sing all a green willow must be my garland.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.54>Let nobody blame him; his scorn I approve,-</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.55>Nay, that's not next.--Hark! who is't that knocks?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech25><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.56>It's the wind.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech26><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.57>[Singing]  I call'd my love false love; but what</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.58>said he then?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.59>Sing willow, willow, willow:</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.60>If I court moe women, you'll couch with moe men!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.61>So, get thee gone; good night Ate eyes do itch;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.62>Doth that bode weeping?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech27><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.63>'Tis neither here nor there.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech28><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.64>I have heard it said so. O, these men, these men!</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.65>Dost thou in conscience think,--tell me, Emilia,--</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.66>That there be women do abuse their husbands</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.67>In such gross kind?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech29><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.68>There be some such, no question.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech30><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.69>Wouldst thou do such a deed for all the world?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech31><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.70>Why, would not you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech32><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.71>No, by this heavenly light!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech33><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.72>Nor I neither by this heavenly light;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.73>I might do't as well i' the dark.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech34><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.74>Wouldst thou do such a deed for all the world?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech35><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.75>The world's a huge thing: it is a great price.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.76>For a small vice.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech36><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.77>In troth, I think thou wouldst not.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech37><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.78>In troth, I think I should; and undo't when I had</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.79>done. Marry, I would not do such a thing for a</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.80>joint-ring, nor for measures of lawn, nor for</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.81>gowns, petticoats, nor caps, nor any petty</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.82>exhibition; but for the whole world,--why, who would</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.83>not make her husband a cuckold to make him a</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.84>monarch? I should venture purgatory for't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech38><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.85>Beshrew me, if I would do such a wrong</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.86>For the whole world.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech39><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.87>Why the wrong is but a wrong i' the world: and</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.88>having the world for your labour, tis a wrong in your</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.89>own world, and you might quickly make it right.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech40><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.90>I do not think there is any such woman.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech41><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.91>Yes, a dozen; and as many to the vantage as would</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.92>store the world they played for.</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.93>But I do think it is their husbands' faults</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.94>If wives do fall: say that they slack their duties,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.95>And pour our treasures into foreign laps,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.96>Or else break out in peevish jealousies,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.97>Throwing restraint upon us; or say they strike us,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.98>Or scant our former having in despite;</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.99>Why, we have galls, and though we have some grace,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.100>Yet have we some revenge. Let husbands know</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.101>Their wives have sense like them: they see and smell</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.102>And have their palates both for sweet and sour,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.103>As husbands have. What is it that they do</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.104>When they change us for others? Is it sport?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.105>I think it is: and doth affection breed it?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.106>I think it doth: is't frailty that thus errs?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.107>It is so too: and have not we affections,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.108>Desires for sport, and frailty, as men have?</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.109>Then let them use us well: else let them know,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.110>The ills we do, their ills instruct us so.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech42><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=4.3.111>Good night, good night: heaven me such uses send,</p>
<p class="line" name=4.3.112>Not to pick bad from bad, but by bad mend!</p>
<p><i>Exeunt</i></p>
</blockquote><p>
<H3>ACT V</h3>
<h3>SCENE I. Cyprus. A street.</h3>
<p><blockquote>
<i>Enter IAGO and RODERIGO</i>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech1><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.1>Here, stand behind this bulk; straight will he come:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.2>Wear thy good rapier bare, and put it home:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.3>Quick, quick; fear nothing; I'll be at thy elbow:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.4>It makes us, or it mars us; think on that,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.5>And fix most firm thy resolution.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech2><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.6>Be near at hand; I may miscarry in't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech3><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.7>Here, at thy hand: be bold, and take thy stand.</p>
<p><i>Retires</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech4><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.8>I have no great devotion to the deed;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.9>And yet he hath given me satisfying reasons:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.10>'Tis but a man gone. Forth, my sword: he dies.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech5><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.11>I have rubb'd this young quat almost to the sense,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.12>And he grows angry. Now, whether he kill Cassio,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.13>Or Cassio him, or each do kill the other,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.14>Every way makes my gain: live Roderigo,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.15>He calls me to a restitution large</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.16>Of gold and jewels that I bobb'd from him,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.17>As gifts to Desdemona;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.18>It must not be: if Cassio do remain,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.19>He hath a daily beauty in his life</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.20>That makes me ugly; and, besides, the Moor</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.21>May unfold me to him; there stand I in much peril:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.22>No, he must die. But so: I hear him coming.</p>
<p><i>Enter CASSIO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech6><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.23>I know his gait, 'tis he.--Villain, thou diest!</p>
<p><i>Makes a pass at CASSIO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech7><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.24>That thrust had been mine enemy indeed,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.25>But that my coat is better than thou know'st</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.26>I will make proof of thine.</p>
<p><i>Draws, and wounds RODERIGO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech8><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.27>O, I am slain!</p>
<p><i>IAGO from behind wounds CASSIO in the leg, and exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech9><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.28>I am maim'd for ever. Help, ho! murder! murder!</p>
<p><i>Falls</i></p>
<p><i>Enter OTHELLO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech10><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.29>The voice of Cassio: Iago keeps his word.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech11><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.30>O, villain that I am!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech12><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.31>It is even so.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech13><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.32>O, help, ho! light! a surgeon!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech14><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.33>'Tis he:--O brave Iago, honest and just,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.34>That hast such noble sense of thy friend's wrong!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.35>Thou teachest me. Minion, your dear lies dead,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.36>And your unblest fate hies: strumpet, I come.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.37>Forth of my heart those charms, thine eyes, are blotted;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.38>Thy bed, lust-stain'd, shall with lust's blood be spotted.</p>
<p><i>Exit</i></p>
<p><i>Enter LODOVICO and GRATIANO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech15><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.39>What, ho! no watch? no passage? murder! murder!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech16><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.40>'Tis some mischance; the cry is very direful.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech17><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.41>O, help!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech18><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.42>Hark!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech19><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.43>O wretched villain!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech20><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.44>Two or three groan: it is a heavy night:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.45>These may be counterfeits: let's think't unsafe</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.46>To come in to the cry without more help.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech21><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.47>Nobody come? then shall I bleed to death.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech22><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.48>Hark!</p>
<p><i>Re-enter IAGO, with a light</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech23><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.49>Here's one comes in his shirt, with light and weapons.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech24><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.50>Who's there? whose noise is this that ones on murder?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech25><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.51>We do not know.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech26><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.52>                  Did not you hear a cry?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech27><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.53>Here, here! for heaven's sake, help me!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech28><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.54>What's the matter?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech29><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.55>This is Othello's ancient, as I take it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech30><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.56>The same indeed; a very valiant fellow.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech31><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.57>What are you here that cry so grievously?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech32><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.58>Iago? O, I am spoil'd, undone by villains!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.59>Give me some help.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech33><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.60>O me, lieutenant! what villains have done this?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech34><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.61>I think that one of them is hereabout,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.62>And cannot make away.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech35><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.63>O treacherous villains!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.64>What are you there? come in, and give some help.</p>
<p><i>To LODOVICO and GRATIANO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech36><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.65>O, help me here!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech37><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.66>That's one of them.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech38><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.67>O murderous slave! O villain!</p>
<p><i>Stabs RODERIGO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech39><b>RODERIGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.68>O damn'd Iago! O inhuman dog!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech40><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.69>Kill men i' the dark!--Where be these bloody thieves?--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.70>How silent is this town!--Ho! murder! murder!--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.71>What may you be? are you of good or evil?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech41><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.72>As you shall prove us, praise us.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech42><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.73>Signior Lodovico?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech43><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.74>He, sir.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech44><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.75>I cry you mercy. Here's Cassio hurt by villains.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech45><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.76>Cassio!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech46><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.77>How is't, brother!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech47><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.78>My leg is cut in two.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech48><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.79>Marry, heaven forbid!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.80>Light, gentlemen; I'll bind it with my shirt.</p>
<p><i>Enter BIANCA</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech49><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.81>What is the matter, ho? who is't that cried?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech50><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.82>Who is't that cried!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech51><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.83>O my dear Cassio! my sweet Cassio! O Cassio,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.84>Cassio, Cassio!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech52><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.85>O notable strumpet! Cassio, may you suspect</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.86>Who they should be that have thus many led you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech53><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.87>No.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech54><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.88>I am to find you thus: I have been to seek you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech55><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.89>Lend me a garter. So. O, for a chair,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.90>To bear him easily hence!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech56><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.91>Alas, he faints! O Cassio, Cassio, Cassio!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech57><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.92>Gentlemen all, I do suspect this trash</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.93>To be a party in this injury.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.94>Patience awhile, good Cassio. Come, come;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.95>Lend me a light. Know we this face or no?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.96>Alas my friend and my dear countryman</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.97>Roderigo! no:--yes, sure: O heaven! Roderigo.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech58><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.98>What, of Venice?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech59><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.99>Even he, sir; did you know him?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech60><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.100>Know him! ay.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech61><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.101>Signior Gratiano? I cry you gentle pardon;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.102>These bloody accidents must excuse my manners,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.103>That so neglected you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech62><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.104>I am glad to see you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech63><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.105>How do you, Cassio? O, a chair, a chair!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech64><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.106>Roderigo!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech65><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.107>He, he 'tis he.</p>
<p><i>A chair brought in</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.108>O, that's well said; the chair!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech66><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.109>Some good man bear him carefully from hence;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.110>I'll fetch the general's surgeon.</p>
<p><i>To BIANCA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.111>For you, mistress,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.112>Save you your labour. He that lies slain</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.113>here, Cassio,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.114>Was my dear friend: what malice was between you?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech67><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.115>None in the world; nor do I know the man.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech68><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.116>[To BIANCA]  What, look you pale? O, bear him out</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.117>o' the air.</p>
<p><i>CASSIO and RODERIGO are borne off</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.118>Stay you, good gentlemen. Look you pale, mistress?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.119>Do you perceive the gastness of her eye?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.120>Nay, if you stare, we shall hear more anon.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.121>Behold her well; I pray you, look upon her:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.122>Do you see, gentlemen? nay, guiltiness will speak,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.123>Though tongues were out of use.</p>
<p><i>Enter EMILIA</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech69><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.124>'Las, what's the matter? what's the matter, husband?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech70><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.125>Cassio hath here been set on in the dark</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.126>By Roderigo and fellows that are scaped:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.127>He's almost slain, and Roderigo dead.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech71><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.128>Alas, good gentleman! alas, good Cassio!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech72><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.129>This is the fruit of whoring. Prithee, Emilia,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.130>Go know of Cassio where he supp'd to-night.</p>
<p><i>To BIANCA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.131>What, do you shake at that?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech73><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.132>He supp'd at my house; but I therefore shake not.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech74><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.133>O, did he so? I charge you, go with me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech75><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.134>Fie, fie upon thee, strumpet!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech76><b>BIANCA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.135>I am no strumpet; but of life as honest</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.136>As you that thus abuse me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech77><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.137>As I! foh! fie upon thee!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech78><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.1.138>Kind gentlemen, let's go see poor Cassio dress'd.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.139>Come, mistress, you must tell's another tale.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.140>Emilia run you to the citadel,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.141>And tell my lord and lady what hath happ'd.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.142>Will you go on? I pray.</p>
<p><i>Aside</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.143>This is the night</p>
<p class="line" name=5.1.144>That either makes me or fordoes me quite.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt</i></p>
</blockquote>
<h3>SCENE II. A bedchamber in the castle: DESDEMONA in bed asleep;</h3>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.1>a light burning.</p>
<p><i>Enter OTHELLO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech1><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.2>It is the cause, it is the cause, my soul,--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.3>Let me not name it to you, you chaste stars!--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.4>It is the cause. Yet I'll not shed her blood;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.5>Nor scar that whiter skin of hers than snow,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.6>And smooth as monumental alabaster.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.7>Yet she must die, else she'll betray more men.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.8>Put out the light, and then put out the light:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.9>If I quench thee, thou flaming minister,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.10>I can again thy former light restore,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.11>Should I repent me: but once put out thy light,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.12>Thou cunning'st pattern of excelling nature,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.13>I know not where is that Promethean heat</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.14>That can thy light relume. When I have pluck'd the rose,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.15>I cannot give it vital growth again.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.16>It must needs wither: I'll smell it on the tree.</p>
<p><i>Kissing her</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.17>Ah balmy breath, that dost almost persuade</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.18>Justice to break her sword! One more, one more.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.19>Be thus when thou art dead, and I will kill thee,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.20>And love thee after. One more, and this the last:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.21>So sweet was ne'er so fatal. I must weep,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.22>But they are cruel tears: this sorrow's heavenly;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.23>It strikes where it doth love. She wakes.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech2><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.24>Who's there? Othello?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech3><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.25>Ay. Desdemona.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech4><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.26>Will you come to bed, my lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech5><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.27>Have you pray'd to-night, Desdemona?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech6><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.28>Ay, my lord.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech7><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.29>If you bethink yourself of any crime</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.30>Unreconciled as yet to heaven and grace,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.31>Solicit for it straight.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech8><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.32>Alas, my lord, what do you mean by that?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech9><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.33>Well, do it, and be brief; I will walk by:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.34>I would not kill thy unprepared spirit;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.35>No; heaven forfend! I would not kill thy soul.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech10><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.36>Talk you of killing?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech11><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.37>Ay, I do.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech12><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.38>Then heaven</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.39>Have mercy on me!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech13><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.40>                  Amen, with all my heart!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech14><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.41>If you say so, I hope you will not kill me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech15><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.42>Hum!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech16><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.43>And yet I fear you; for you are fatal then</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.44>When your eyes roll so: why I should fear I know not,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.45>Since guiltiness I know not; but yet I feel I fear.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech17><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.46>Think on thy sins.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech18><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.47>                  They are loves I bear to you.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech19><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.48>Ay, and for that thou diest.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech20><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.49>That death's unnatural that kills for loving.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.50>Alas, why gnaw you so your nether lip?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.51>Some bloody passion shakes your very frame:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.52>These are portents; but yet I hope, I hope,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.53>They do not point on me.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech21><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.54>Peace, and be still!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech22><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.55>I will so. What's the matter?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech23><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.56>That handkerchief which I so loved and gave thee</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.57>Thou gavest to Cassio.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech24><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.58>No, by my life and soul!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.59>Send for the man, and ask him.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech25><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.60>Sweet soul, take heed,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.61>Take heed of perjury; thou art on thy deathbed.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech26><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.62>Ay, but not yet to die.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech27><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.63>Yes, presently:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.64>Therefore confess thee freely of thy sin;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.65>For to deny each article with oath</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.66>Cannot remove nor choke the strong conception</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.67>That I do groan withal. Thou art to die.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech28><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.68>Then Lord have mercy on me!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech29><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.69>I say, amen.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech30><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.70>And have you mercy too! I never did</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.71>Offend you in my life; never loved Cassio</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.72>But with such general warranty of heaven</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.73>As I might love: I never gave him token.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech31><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.74>By heaven, I saw my handkerchief in's hand.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.75>O perjured woman! thou dost stone my heart,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.76>And makest me call what I intend to do</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.77>A murder, which I thought a sacrifice:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.78>I saw the handkerchief.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech32><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.79>He found it then;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.80>I never gave it him: send for him hither;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.81>Let him confess a truth.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech33><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.82>He hath confess'd.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech34><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.83>What, my lord?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech35><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.84>That he hath used thee.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech36><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.85>How? unlawfully?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech37><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.86>Ay.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech38><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.87>He will not say so.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech39><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.88>No, his mouth is stopp'd;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.89>Honest Iago hath ta'en order for't.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech40><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.90>O! my fear interprets: what, is he dead?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech41><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.91>Had all his hairs been lives, my great revenge</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.92>Had stomach for them all.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech42><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.93>Alas! he is betray'd and I undone.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech43><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.94>Out, strumpet! weep'st thou for him to my face?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech44><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.95>O, banish me, my lord, but kill me not!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech45><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.96>Down, strumpet!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech46><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.97>Kill me to-morrow: let me live to-night!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech47><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.98>Nay, if you strive--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech48><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.99>But half an hour!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech49><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.100>                  Being done, there is no pause.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech50><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.101>But while I say one prayer!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech51><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.102>It is too late.</p>
<p><i>He stifles her</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech52><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.103>[Within]  My lord , my lord! what, ho! my lord, my lord!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech53><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.104>What noise is this? Not dead? not yet quite dead?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.105>I that am cruel am yet merciful;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.106>I would not have thee linger in thy pain: So, so.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech54><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.107>[Within]  What, ho! my lord, my lord!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech55><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.108>Who's there?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech56><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.109>[Within]  O, good my lord, I would speak a word with you!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech57><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.110>Yes: 'tis Emilia. By and by. She's dead.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.111>'Tis like she comes to speak of Cassio's death.--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.112>The noise was here. Ha! no more moving?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.113>Still as the grave. Shall she come in? were't good?--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.114>I think she stirs again:--no. What's best to do?</p>
