<p class="line" name=5.2.115>If she come in, she'll sure speak to my wife:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.116>My wife! my wife! what wife? I have no wife.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.117>O insupportable! O heavy hour!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.118>Methinks it should be now a huge eclipse</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.119>Of sun and moon, and that the affrighted globe</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.120>Should yawn at alteration.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech58><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.121>[Within]  I do beseech you</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.122>That I may speak with you, O, good my lord!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech59><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.123>I had forgot thee: O, come in, Emilia;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.124>Soft; by and by. Let me the curtains draw.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.125>Where art thou?</p>
<p><i>Unlocks the door</i></p>
<p><i>Enter EMILIA</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.126>What's the matter with thee now?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech60><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.127>O, my good lord, yonder's foul murders done!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech61><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.128>What, now?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech62><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.129>But now, my lord.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech63><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.130>It is the very error of the moon;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.131>She comes more nearer earth than she was wont,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.132>And makes men mad.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech64><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.133>Cassio, my lord, hath kill'd a young Venetian</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.134>Call'd Roderigo.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech65><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.135>                  Roderigo kill'd!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.136>And Cassio kill'd!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech66><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.137>No, Cassio is not kill'd.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech67><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.138>Not Cassio kill'd! then murder's out of tune,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.139>And sweet revenge grows harsh.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech68><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.140>O, falsely, falsely murder'd!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech69><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.141>Alas, what cry is that?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech70><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.142>That! what?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech71><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.143>Out, and alas! that was my lady's voice.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.144>Help! help, ho! help! O lady, speak again!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.145>Sweet Desdemona! O sweet mistress, speak!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech72><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.146>A guiltless death I die.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech73><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.147>O, who hath done this deed?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech74><b>DESDEMONA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.148>Nobody; I myself. Farewell</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.149>Commend me to my kind lord: O, farewell!</p>
<p><i>Dies</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech75><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.150>Why, how should she be murder'd?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech76><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.151>Alas, who knows?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech77><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.152>You heard her say herself, it was not I.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech78><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.153>She said so: I must needs report the truth.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech79><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.154>She's, like a liar, gone to burning hell:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.155>'Twas I that kill'd her.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech80><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.156>O, the more angel she,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.157>And you the blacker devil!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech81><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.158>She turn'd to folly, and she was a whore.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech82><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.159>Thou dost belie her, and thou art a devil.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech83><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.160>She was false as water.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech84><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.161>Thou art rash as fire, to say</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.162>That she was false: O, she was heavenly true!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech85><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.163>Cassio did top her; ask thy husband else.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.164>O, I were damn'd beneath all depth in hell,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.165>But that I did proceed upon just grounds</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.166>To this extremity. Thy husband knew it all.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech86><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.167>My husband!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech87><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.168>Thy husband.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech88><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.169>That she was false to wedlock?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech89><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.170>Ay, with Cassio. Nay, had she been true,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.171>If heaven would make me such another world</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.172>Of one entire and Perfect chrysolite,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.173>I'ld not have sold her for it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech90><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.174>My husband!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech91><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.175>          Ay, 'twas he that told me first:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.176>An honest man he is, and hates the slime</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.177>That sticks on filthy deeds.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech92><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.178>My husband!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech93><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.179>What needs this iteration, woman? I say thy husband.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech94><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.180>O mistress, villany hath made mocks with love,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.181>My husband say that she was false!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech95><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.182>He, woman;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.183>I say thy husband: dost understand the word?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.184>My friend, thy husband, honest, honest Iago.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech96><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.185>If he say so, may his pernicious soul</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.186>Rot half a grain a day! he lies to the heart:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.187>She was too fond of her most filthy bargain.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech97><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.188>Ha!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech98><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.189>Do thy worst:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.190>This deed of thine is no more worthy heaven</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.191>Than thou wast worthy her.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech99><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.192>Peace, you were best.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech100><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.193>Thou hast not half that power to do me harm</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.194>As I have to be hurt. O gull! O dolt!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.195>As ignorant as dirt! thou hast done a deed--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.196>I care not for thy sword; I'll make thee known,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.197>Though I lost twenty lives.--Help! help, ho! help!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.198>The Moor hath kill'd my mistress! Murder! murder!</p>
<p><i>Enter MONTANO, GRATIANO, IAGO, and others</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech101><b>MONTANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.199>What is the matter? How now, general!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech102><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.200>O, are you come, Iago? you have done well,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.201>That men must lay their murders on your neck.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech103><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.202>What is the matter?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech104><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.203>Disprove this villain, if thou be'st a man:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.204>He says thou told'st him that his wife was false:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.205>I know thou didst not, thou'rt not such a villain:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.206>Speak, for my heart is full.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech105><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.207>I told him what I thought, and told no more</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.208>Than what he found himself was apt and true.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech106><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.209>But did you ever tell him she was false?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech107><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.210>I did.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech108><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.211>You told a lie, an odious, damned lie;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.212>Upon my soul, a lie, a wicked lie.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.213>She false with Cassio!--did you say with Cassio?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech109><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.214>With Cassio, mistress. Go to, charm your tongue.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech110><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.215>I will not charm my tongue; I am bound to speak:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.216>My mistress here lies murder'd in her bed,--</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech111><b>All</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.217>O heavens forfend!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech112><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.218>And your reports have set the murder on.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech113><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.219>Nay, stare not, masters: it is true, indeed.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech114><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.220>'Tis a strange truth.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech115><b>MONTANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.221>O monstrous act!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech116><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.222>                  Villany, villany, villany!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.223>I think upon't, I think: I smell't: O villany!--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.224>I thought so then:--I'll kill myself for grief:--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.225>O villany, villany!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech117><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.226>What, are you mad? I charge you, get you home.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech118><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.227>Good gentlemen, let me have leave to speak:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.228>'Tis proper I obey him, but not now.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.229>Perchance, Iago, I will ne'er go home.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech119><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.230>O! O! O!</p>
<p><i>He falls on the bed</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech120><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.231>       Nay, lay thee down and roar;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.232>For thou hast kill'd the sweetest innocent</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.233>That e'er did lift up eye.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech121><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.234>[Rising]  O, she was foul!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.235>I scarce did know you, uncle: there lies your niece,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.236>Whose breath, indeed, these hands have newly stopp'd:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.237>I know this act shows horrible and grim.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech122><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.238>Poor Desdemona! I am glad thy father's dead:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.239>Thy match was mortal to him, and pure grief</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.240>Shore his old thread in twain: did he live now,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.241>This sight would make him do a desperate turn,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.242>Yea, curse his better angel from his side,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.243>And fall to reprobation.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech123><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.244>'Tis pitiful; but yet Iago knows</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.245>That she with Cassio hath the act of shame</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.246>A thousand times committed; Cassio confess'd it:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.247>And she did gratify his amorous works</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.248>With that recognizance and pledge of love</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.249>Which I first gave her; I saw it in his hand:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.250>It was a handkerchief, an antique token</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.251>My father gave my mother.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech124><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.252>O heaven! O heavenly powers!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech125><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.253>Come, hold your peace.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech126><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.254>'Twill out, 'twill out: I peace!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.255>No, I will speak as liberal as the north:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.256>Let heaven and men and devils, let them all,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.257>All, all, cry shame against me, yet I'll speak.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech127><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.258>Be wise, and get you home.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech128><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.259>I will not.</p>
<p><i>IAGO offers to stab EMILIA</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech129><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.260>Fie!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.261>Your sword upon a woman?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech130><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.262>O thou dull Moor! that handkerchief thou speak'st of</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.263>I found by fortune and did give my husband;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.264>For often, with a solemn earnestness,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.265>More than indeed belong'd to such a trifle,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.266>He begg'd of me to steal it.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech131><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.267>Villanous whore!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech132><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.268>She give it Cassio! no, alas! I found it,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.269>And I did give't my husband.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech133><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.270>Filth, thou liest!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech134><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.271>By heaven, I do not, I do not, gentlemen.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.272>O murderous coxcomb! what should such a fool</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.273>Do with so good a woman?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech135><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.274>Are there no stones in heaven</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.275>But what serve for the thunder?--Precious villain!</p>
<p><i>He runs at IAGO  IAGO, from behind, stabs EMILIA, and exit</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech136><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.276>The woman falls; sure, he hath kill'd his wife.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech137><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.277>Ay, ay: O, lay me by my mistress' side.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech138><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.278>He's gone, but his wife's kill'd.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech139><b>MONTANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.279>'Tis a notorious villain. Take you this weapon,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.280>Which I have here recover'd from the Moor:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.281>Come, guard the door without; let him not pass,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.282>But kill him rather. I'll after that same villain,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.283>For 'tis a damned slave.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt MONTANO and GRATIANO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech140><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.284>I am not valiant neither,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.285>But ever puny whipster gets my sword:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.286>But why should honour outlive honesty?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.287>Let it go all.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech141><b>EMILIA</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.288>What did thy song bode, lady?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.289>Hark, canst thou hear me? I will play the swan.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.290>And die in music.</p>
<p><i>Singing</i></p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.291>Willow, willow, willow,--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.292>Moor, she was chaste; she loved thee, cruel Moor;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.293>So come my soul to bliss, as I speak true;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.294>So speaking as I think, I die, I die.</p>
<p><i>Dies</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech142><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.295>I have another weapon in this chamber;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.296>It is a sword of Spain, the ice-brook's temper:--</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.297>O, here it is. Uncle, I must come forth.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech143><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.298>[Within]  If thou attempt it, it will cost thee dear:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.299>Thou hast no weapon, and perforce must suffer.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech144><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.300>Look in upon me then and speak with me,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.301>Or, naked as I am, I will assault thee.</p>
<p><i>Re-enter GRATIANO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech145><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.302>What is the matter?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech146><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.303>Behold, I have a weapon;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.304>A better never did itself sustain</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.305>Upon a soldier's thigh: I have seen the day,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.306>That, with this little arm and this good sword,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.307>I have made my way through more impediments</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.308>Than twenty times your stop: but, O vain boast!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.309>Who can control his fate? 'tis not so now.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.310>Be not afraid, though you do see me weapon'd;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.311>Here is my journey's end, here is my butt,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.312>And very sea-mark of my utmost sail.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.313>Do you go back dismay'd? 'tis a lost fear;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.314>Man but a rush against Othello's breast,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.315>And he retires. Where should Othello go?</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.316>Now, how dost thou look now? O ill-starr'd wench!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.317>Pale as thy smock! when we shall meet at compt,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.318>This look of thine will hurl my soul from heaven,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.319>And fiends will snatch at it. Cold, cold, my girl!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.320>Even like thy chastity. O cursed slave!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.321>Whip me, ye devils,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.322>From the possession of this heavenly sight!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.323>Blow me about in winds! roast me in sulphur!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.324>Wash me in steep-down gulfs of liquid fire!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.325>O Desdemona! Desdemona! dead!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.326>Oh! Oh! Oh!</p>
<p><i>Enter LODOVICO. MONTANO, CASSIO carried in a chair, and Officers with IAGO, prisoner</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech147><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.327>Where is this rash and most unfortunate man?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech148><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.328>That's he that was Othello: here I am.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech149><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.329>Where is that viper? bring the villain forth.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech150><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.330>I look down towards his feet; but that's a fable.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.331>If that thou best a devil, I cannot kill thee.</p>
<p><i>Wounds IAGO</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech151><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.332>Wrench his sword from him.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech152><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.333>I bleed, sir; but not kill'd.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech153><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.334>I am not sorry neither: I'ld have thee live;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.335>For, in my sense, 'tis happiness to die.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech154><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.336>O thou Othello, thou wert once so good,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.337>Fall'n in the practise of a damned slave,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.338>What shall be said to thee?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech155><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.339>Why, any thing:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.340>An honourable murderer, if you will;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.341>For nought I did in hate, but all in honour.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech156><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.342>This wretch hath part confess'd his villany:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.343>Did you and he consent in Cassio's death?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech157><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.344>Ay.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech158><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.345>Dear general, I never gave you cause.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech159><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.346>I do believe it, and I ask your pardon.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.347>Will you, I pray, demand that demi-devil</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.348>Why he hath thus ensnared my soul and body?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech160><b>IAGO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.349>Demand me nothing: what you know, you know:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.350>From this time forth I never will speak word.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech161><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.351>What, not to pray?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech162><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.352>                  Torments will ope your lips.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech163><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.353>Well, thou dost best.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech164><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.354>Sir, you shall understand what hath befall'n,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.355>Which, as I think, you know not. Here is a letter</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.356>Found in the pocket of the slain Roderigo;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.357>And here another: the one of them imports</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.358>The death of Cassio to be undertook</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.359>By Roderigo.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech165><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.360>O villain!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech166><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.361>Most heathenish and most gross!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech167><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.362>Now here's another discontented paper,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.363>Found in his pocket too; and this, it seems,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.364>Roderigo meant to have sent this damned villain;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.365>But that belike Iago in the interim</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.366>Came in and satisfied him.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech168><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.367>O the pernicious caitiff!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.368>How came you, Cassio, by that handkerchief</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.369>That was my wife's?</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech169><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.370>I found it in my chamber:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.371>And he himself confess'd but even now</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.372>That there he dropp'd it for a special purpose</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.373>Which wrought to his desire.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech170><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.374>O fool! fool! fool!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech171><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.375>There is besides in Roderigo's letter,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.376>How he upbraids Iago, that he made him</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.377>Brave me upon the watch; whereon it came</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.378>That I was cast: and even but now he spake,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.379>After long seeming dead, Iago hurt him,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.380>Iago set him on.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech172><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.381>You must forsake this room, and go with us:</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.382>Your power and your command is taken off,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.383>And Cassio rules in Cyprus. For this slave,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.384>If there be any cunning cruelty</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.385>That can torment him much and hold him long,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.386>It shall be his. You shall close prisoner rest,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.387>Till that the nature of your fault be known</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.388>To the Venetian state. Come, bring him away.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech173><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.389>Soft you; a word or two before you go.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.390>I have done the state some service, and they know't.</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.391>No more of that. I pray you, in your letters,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.392>When you shall these unlucky deeds relate,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.393>Speak of me as I am; nothing extenuate,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.394>Nor set down aught in malice: then must you speak</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.395>Of one that loved not wisely but too well;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.396>Of one not easily jealous, but being wrought</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.397>Perplex'd in the extreme; of one whose hand,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.398>Like the base Indian, threw a pearl away</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.399>Richer than all his tribe; of one whose subdued eyes,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.400>Albeit unused to the melting mood,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.401>Drop tears as fast as the Arabian trees</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.402>Their medicinal gum. Set you down this;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.403>And say besides, that in Aleppo once,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.404>Where a malignant and a turban'd Turk</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.405>Beat a Venetian and traduced the state,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.406>I took by the throat the circumcised dog,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.407>And smote him, thus.</p>
<p><i>Stabs himself</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech174><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.408>O bloody period!</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech175><b>GRATIANO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.409>                  All that's spoke is marr'd.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech176><b>OTHELLO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.410>I kiss'd thee ere I kill'd thee: no way but this;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.411>Killing myself, to die upon a kiss.</p>
<p><i>Falls on the bed, and dies</i></p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech177><b>CASSIO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.412>This did I fear, but thought he had no weapon;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.413>For he was great of heart.</p>
</blockquote>

<p class="line" name=speech178><b>LODOVICO</b></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="line" name=5.2.414>[To IAGO]  O Spartan dog,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.415>More fell than anguish, hunger, or the sea!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.416>Look on the tragic loading of this bed;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.417>This is thy work: the object poisons sight;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.418>Let it be hid. Gratiano, keep the house,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.419>And seize upon the fortunes of the Moor,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.420>For they succeed on you. To you, lord governor,</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.421>Remains the censure of this hellish villain;</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.422>The time, the place, the torture: O, enforce it!</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.423>Myself will straight aboard: and to the state</p>
<p class="line" name=5.2.424>This heavy act with heavy heart relate.</p>
<p><i>Exeunt</i></p>
